DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS NEGOCIOS;
CREATE DATABASE NEGOCIOS;

USE NEGOCIOS;

CREATE TABLE CATEGORIA (
  IDE_CAT 	INT 		NOT NULL auto_increment,
  NOM_CAT	VARCHAR(15) 	NOT NULL,
  DES_CAT	VARCHAR(100),
  PRIMARY KEY(IDE_CAT)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE PROVEEDOR (
  IDE_PROV 	INT 			NOT NULL auto_increment,
  NOM_PROV 	VARCHAR(40) 	NOT NULL,
  NOM_CONT 	VARCHAR(80) 	NOT NULL,
  CAR_CONT 	VARCHAR(50) 	NOT NULL,
  DIR_PROV 	VARCHAR(60) 	NOT NULL,
  IDE_PAI 	INT	 			NOT NULL,
  FON_PROV 	VARCHAR(15) 	NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(IDE_PROV),
  FOREIGN KEY (IDE_PAI) REFERENCES PAIS(IDE_PAI)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE PRODUCTO (
  IDE_PRO	INT 		NOT NULL auto_increment,
  NOM_PRO 	VARCHAR(40) NOT NULL,
  IDE_PROV 	INT 		NOT NULL,
  IDE_CAT 	INT 		NOT NULL,
  CXU_PRO 	VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
  PRE_PRO 	DECIMAL(10,2) 	NOT NULL,
  UEX_PRO 	INT 		NOT NULL,
  UPE_PRO	INT 		NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(IDE_PRO),
  FOREIGN KEY(IDE_PROV) REFERENCES PROVEEDOR(IDE_PROV),
  FOREIGN KEY(IDE_CAT) REFERENCES CATEGORIA(IDE_CAT)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE CARGO(
	IDE_CAR INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
	DES_CAR VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(IDE_CAR)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

INSERT CARGO VALUES(1,'REPRESENTANTE DE VENTA');
INSERT CARGO VALUES(2,'EJECUTIVO DE VENTA');
INSERT CARGO VALUES(3,'SUPERVISOR DE VENTA');
INSERT CARGO VALUES(4,'AUXILIAR DE VENTA');

CREATE TABLE DISTRITO(
	IDE_DIS INT NOT NULL,
	NOM_DIS VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY(IDE_DIS)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

INSERT DISTRITO VALUES(1,'LIMA');
INSERT DISTRITO VALUES(2,'RIMAC');
INSERT DISTRITO VALUES(3,'ATE');
INSERT DISTRITO VALUES(4,'SAN MIGUEL');

CREATE TABLE EMPLEADO (
  IDE_EMP INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
  APE_EMP VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  NOM_EMP VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  FNA_EMP DATE NOT NULL,
  DIR_EMP VARCHAR(60) NOT NULL,
  IDE_DIS INT REFERENCES DISTRITO,
  FON_EMP VARCHAR(15) NULL,
  IDE_CAR INT REFERENCES CARGO,
  FCO_EMP DATE NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY(IDE_EMP),
  FOREIGN KEY(IDE_DIS) REFERENCES DISTRITO(IDE_DIS),
  FOREIGN KEY(IDE_CAR) REFERENCES CARGO(IDE_CAR)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE PEDIDO(
	IDE_PED INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
	IDE_CLI INT NULL ,
	IDE_EMP INT NULL,
	FEC_PED DATE NOT NULL,
	FEN_PED DATE NULL,
	FEE_PED DATE NULL,
	ENV_PED CHAR(1) NULL DEFAULT 0,
	CAN_PED INT NULL,
	DES_PED VARCHAR(40) NULL,
	DDE_PED VARCHAR(60) NULL,
	CDE_PED VARCHAR(60) NULL,
	REF_PED VARCHAR(60) NULL,
	DEP_PED VARCHAR(60) NULL,
	PAI_PED VARCHAR(60) NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY(IDE_PED),
	FOREIGN KEY(IDE_CLI) REFERENCES CLIENTE(IDE_CLI),
	FOREIGN KEY(IDE_EMP) REFERENCES EMPLEADO(IDE_EMP)
)ENGINE = InnoDB;

CREATE TABLE DETALLE(
	IDE_PED INT NOT NULL ,
	IDE_PRO INT NOT NULL,
	PRE_DET DECIMAL(10, 0) NOT NULL,
	CAN_DET INT NOT NULL,
	DES_DET DECIMAL NOT NULL,
	PRIMARY KEY(IDE_PED,IDE_PRO) ,
	FOREIGN KEY(IDE_PED) REFERENCES PEDIDO(IDE_PED),
	FOREIGN KEY(IDE_PRO) REFERENCES PRODUCTO(IDE_PRO) 
)ENGINE = InnoDB;
